      '\r\n' +

      '\r\n' +
      'Chapter "B Generic UART" in "ARM Server Base System Architecture" [1]\r\n' +
      'documentation describes a generic UART interface. Such generic UART\r\n' +

  {
    title: 'CVE-2022-50626 In the Linux kernel, the following vulnerability has been resolved\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'media dvb-usb fix memory leak...',
    link: 'https//nvd.nist.gov/vuln/detail/CVE-2022-50626',
    pubDate: 'Mon, 08 Dec 2025 02:15:00 GMT',
    content: '![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[In the Linux kernel, the following vulnerability has been resolved\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'media dvb-usb fix memory leak in dvb_usb_adapter_init()\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'Syzbot reports a memory leak in "dvb_usb_adapter_init()".\r\n' +
      "The leak is due to not accounting for and freeing current iteration's\r\n" +
      'adapter->priv in case of an error. Currently if an error occurs,\r\n' +
      'it will exit before incrementing "num_adapters_initalized",\r\n' +
      'which is used as a reference counter to free all adap->priv\r\n' +
      'in "dvb_usb_adapter_exit()". There are multiple error paths that\r\n' +
      'can exit from before incrementing the counter. Including the\r\n' +
      'error handling paths for "dvb_usb_adapter_stream_init()",\r\n' +
      '"dvb_usb_adapter_dvb_init()" and "dvb_usb_adapter_frontend_init()"\r\n' +
      'within "dvb_usb_adapter_init()".\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'This means that in case of an error in any of these functions the\r\n' +
      "current iteration is not accounted for and the current iteration's\r\n" +
      'adap->priv is not freed.\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      "Fix this by freeing the current iteration's adap->priv in the\r\n" +
      '"stream_init_err" label in the error path. The rest of the\r\n' +
      '(accounted for) adap->priv objects are freed in dvb_usb_adapter_exit()\r\n' +
      'as expected using the num_adapters_initalized variable.\r\n' +

    contentSnippet: '![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[In the Linux kernel, the following vulnerability has been resolved\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'media dvb-usb fix memory leak in dvb_usb_adapter_init()\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'Syzbot reports a memory leak in "dvb_usb_adapter_init()".\r\n' +
      "The leak is due to not accounting for and freeing current iteration's\r\n" +
      'adapter->priv in case of an error. Currently if an error occurs,\r\n' +
      'it will exit before incrementing "num_adapters_initalized",\r\n' +
      'which is used as a reference counter to free all adap->priv\r\n' +
      'in "dvb_usb_adapter_exit()". There are multiple error paths that\r\n' +
      'can exit from before incrementing the counter. Including the\r\n' +
      'error handling paths for "dvb_usb_adapter_stream_init()",\r\n' +
      '"dvb_usb_adapter_dvb_init()" and "dvb_usb_adapter_frontend_init()"\r\n' +
      'within "dvb_usb_adapter_init()".\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'This means that in case of an error in any of these functions the\r\n' +
      "current iteration is not accounted for and the current iteration's\r\n" +
      'adap->priv is not freed.\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      "Fix this by freeing the current iteration's adap->priv in the\r\n" +
      '"stream_init_err" label in the error path. The rest of the\r\n' +
      '(accounted for) adap->priv objects are freed in dvb_usb_adapter_exit()\r\n' +
      'as expected using the num_adapters_initalized variable.\r\n' +

      '\r\n' +
      'The vma_lock and hugetlb_fault_mutex are dropped before handling userfault\r\n' +
      'and reacquire them again after handle_userfault(), but reacquire the\r\n' +
      'vma_lock could lead to UAF[1,2] due to the following race,\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'hugetlb_fault\r\n' +

      '                                             do_mmap\r\n' +
      '                                               mmap_region\r\n' +
      '                                                 munmap_vma_range\r\n' +
      '                                                   /* clean old vma */\r\n' +
      '        /* lock vma_lock again  --- UAF */\r\n' +
      '    /* unlock vma_lock */\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'Since the vma_lock will unlock immediately after\r\n' +
      "hugetlb_handle_userfault(), let's drop the unneeded lock and unlock in\r\n" +
